  <script type="text/javascript">
   (function SSLredirect(){ 
	if(window.location.protocol != "http:"){return} 
	var globalNavCookie; 
	var allCookies = document.cookie.split('; '); 
	var httpsPort = "443"; 
	for (var i=0;i&lt;allCookies.length;i++) { 
		var cookiePair = allCookies[i].split('='); 
		var cookieName = cookiePair[0]; 
		cookiePair.shift(); 
		var cookieValue = cookiePair.join('='); 
		if(cookieName == "GNSESS"){globalNavCookie = new Function("return " + cookieValue)()} 
	} 
	if(typeof globalNavCookie == "object" &amp;&amp; typeof globalNavCookie.ENC != "undefined" &amp;&amp; globalNavCookie.ENC != ""){ 
		var newUrl = document.createElement('a'); 
		if(httpsPort != ""){newUrl.port = httpsPort} 
		newUrl.href = window.location.href; 
		newUrl.protocol = "https"; 
		window.location.href = newUrl.href; 
	} 
})();
  </script>

  <script>
   var uagent = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase(); 
	function getURLParam(pName) { 
		var queryString = location.search, startPos, stopPos, tempPos = 0, pValue = ""; 
		if (typeof pName === "string" &amp;&amp; pName !== "") { 
			if (queryString.indexOf(pName) != -1) { 
				startPos = queryString.indexOf(pName) + pName.length + 1; 
				stopPos = ((tempPos = (queryString.indexOf("&amp;", startPos))) == -1) ? queryString.length : tempPos; 
				return unescape(queryString.substring(startPos, stopPos)); 
			} 
		} 
		return pValue; 
	} 
	function setOrderSourceABSplit() { 
		var referrer = document.referrer; 
		if(referrer.indexOf("/login") == -1 &amp;&amp; (referrer.indexOf("/shopmobile/") != -1 || referrer.indexOf('http://m.att.com') != -1)){ 
			var ajaxUrl = location.pathname.replace('.html', '.setOrderSourceABSplit.xhr.html'); 
			var request = new XMLHttpRequest(); 
			request.open("GET",ajaxUrl,true); 
			request.send(); 
			sessionStorage.setItem("storageFullSiteView", "True"); 
			return true; 
		} 
		return false; 
	} 
	if (getURLParam("mobile") === "false") { 
		sessionStorage.setItem("storageFullSiteView", "True"); 
		setOrderSourceABSplit(); 
	} else { 
		if(typeof(Storage) === "undefined" || sessionStorage.getItem("storageFullSiteView") !== "True" &amp;&amp; !setOrderSourceABSplit()) { 
			if (uagent.indexOf("mobile") &gt; -1) { 
				if (uagent.indexOf("ipad") &lt; 0 &amp;&amp; uagent.indexOf("tablet") &lt; 0 &amp;&amp; uagent.indexOf("gt-p10") &lt; 0) { 
					var ajaxUrl = location.pathname.replace('.html', '.sessioninvalidate.html'); 
					var request = new XMLHttpRequest(); 
					var referrer = encodeURIComponent(document.referrer); 
					request.open("GET",ajaxUrl,true); 
					request.send(); 
					referrer = referrer.replace("%3A","%253A"); 
					if (window.location.search != '') { 
						window.location = "http://m.att.com/shopmobile/wireless/devices/smartphones.html?taxoManu=LG&amp;.html" + window.location.search + '&amp;referrer=' + referrer; 
					} else { 
						window.location = "http://m.att.com/shopmobile/wireless/devices/smartphones.html?taxoManu=LG&amp;.html" + '?referrer=' + referrer; 
					} 
				} 
			} 
		} 
	}
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function processCompareDevices(inStr) {	 
		var params = []; 
		var compareDevicesUrl = "/devices/comparephone.html"; 
		var commitmentTerm = jQuery("input.listFilterGroup[name=commitmentTerm]:checked").val() || "0"; 
		var allCheckboxesToProcess = jQuery("input[name=skuId]:checked"); 
		var allCheckboxesToProcessSize = allCheckboxesToProcess.size(); 
		if (allCheckboxesToProcessSize == 0) { 
			jQuery("a#compareUrl").attr("href", function() { 
				return compareDevicesUrl; 
			});	 
		} else { 
			if (allCheckboxesToProcessSize &gt; 5) { 
				//currentMessage = jQuery("div#yellowMessage").html(); 
				//var compareErrorMsg = "You selected " + allCheckboxesToProcessSize + " devices to compare. The maximum is 5. You will not be redirected."; 
			} else { 
				params = allCheckboxesToProcess.map(function() {return "sku=" + jQuery(this).val()}).get() || []; 
				if(commitmentTerm.toLowerCase() != "all") {params.push("term=" + commitmentTerm)}; 
				jQuery("a#compareUrl").attr("href", function() {return compareDevicesUrl + "?" + params.join("&amp;")}); 
			} 
		} 
	} 
	//RTI sku WT tags 
	jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 
		ATT.cqWebtrend.wtRTISku(); 
		ATT.cqWebtrend.wtRTIOther(); 
	});
  </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var atgProfileDataReady = jQuery.Deferred(); 
    $CQ(function() { 
    	//delete itmes with "_XSS" names  
        if(window.localStorage!==undefined){  
            var strData = decodeURIComponent(window.localStorage.getItem("ClientSidePersistence"));  
            if(strData.toLowerCase().indexOf("_xss") &gt; -1){  
                var arrData = strData.split("%2C");  
                var strClientPersistance = "";  
                for(var i=0;i&lt;arrData.length;i++)  
                {  
                    if(arrData[i].toLowerCase().indexOf("_xss") &gt; -1){  
                        continue;  
                    }  
                    else{  
                       strClientPersistance += arrData[i];  
                    }  
                }  
                window.localStorage.setItem("ClientSidePersistence",encodeURIComponent(strClientPersistance));  
            }  
        } 
    	// call to att profile 
        loadATTProfileForPersonalization(); 
        CQ_Analytics.SegmentMgr.loadSegments("/shopcms/shopetc/segmentation"); 
	        CQ_Analytics.ClientContextUtils.init("/shopcms/shopetc/clientcontext/default","/shop/wireless/devices/lg"); 
    }); 
    // method to make ajax call to atgprofile to get a json and set in the SessionPersistence cookie or Localstorage 
    function loadATTProfileForPersonalization() 
     { 
         atgProfileDataReady; 
 		var atgProfileDataTimer = setTimeout(function() { 
 		atgProfileDataReady.reject();  
 		}, 4000); 
 	//setting authorizaleId with our trustedkey for fixing the errors.		 
     CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty("authorizableId", "03e2a1cac921ba5da75666813d03996c"); 
	    var v_orderCookie = ATT.util.getCookie('ORDER_COOKIE'); 
        console.log("DEBUG : Order cookie read - " + v_orderCookie); 
	    if(v_orderCookie) { 
            console.log("DEBUG : Order cookie read is - " + v_orderCookie); 
	        var v_orderCookieJson = jQuery.parseJSON(v_orderCookie); 
	        var orderDate = v_orderCookieJson.orderSubmittedDate; 
	        console.log("DEBUG : orderDate from cookie = " + orderDate); 
	        if(orderDate!=null){ 
                var yy = parseInt(orderDate.substring(0,4)); 
                var mm = parseInt(orderDate.substring(5,7))-1; 
                var dd = parseInt(orderDate.substring(8,10)); 
                if(!isNaN(yy) &amp;&amp; !isNaN(mm) &amp;&amp; !isNaN(dd)){ 
		            var orderDateDate = new Date(yy,mm,dd,0,0,0,0); 
	                console.log("DEBUG : orderDateDate = " + orderDateDate); 
					var currentDate = new Date(); 
	                console.log("DEBUG : currentDate = " + currentDate); 
		            if(orderDateDate!=null &amp;&amp; currentDate!=null){ 
		                var timeDiff = Math.abs(currentDate.getTime() - orderDateDate.getTime()); 
						var diffDays = Math.ceil(timeDiff / (1000 * 3600 * 24));  
	                    console.log("DEBUG : diffDays = " + diffDays); 
		                if(diffDays&gt;0){ 
							CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty('daysSinceLastOrderSubmitted', diffDays);       
		                } 
		            } 
		        } 
	        } else { 
	        	CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty('daysSinceLastOrderSubmitted', -1);  
	        } 
	    } 
    	$CQ.ajax({ url: '/shop/wireless/devices/lg/_jcr_content.atgprofile.xhr.json', cache: false, dataType: 'text', success: function(data){ 
 		var json = jQuery.parseJSON(data);	 
        var contextFromLS = unescape(window.localStorage.getItem("ClientSidePersistence")); 
        var start = contextFromLS.indexOf("checkAvailabilityPerformed="); 
        var end = 0; 
        if(start&gt;0) end = contextFromLS.indexOf(",",start); 
		var capFromLS = "N"; 
        if(start&gt;0 &amp;&amp; end!=0) capFromLS = contextFromLS.substring(start+27, end); 
        start = contextFromLS.indexOf("addressLine1="); 
        end = 0; 
        if(start&gt;0) end = contextFromLS.indexOf(",",start); 
		var addressLine1FromLS = ""; 
        if(start&gt;0 &amp;&amp; end!=0) addressLine1FromLS = contextFromLS.substring(start+13, end);             
        start = contextFromLS.indexOf("zip5="); 
        end = 0; 
        if(start&gt;0) end = contextFromLS.indexOf(",",start); 
		var zip5 = ""; 
        if(start&gt;0 &amp;&amp; end!=0) zip5 = contextFromLS.substring(start+5, end);       
        start = contextFromLS.indexOf("zip="); 
        end = 0; 
        if(start&gt;0) end = contextFromLS.indexOf(",",start); 
		var zip = ""; 
        if(start&gt;0 &amp;&amp; end!=0) zip = contextFromLS.substring(start+4, end);  
        start = contextFromLS.indexOf("paperlessFlag="); 
        end = 0; 
        if(start&gt;0) end = contextFromLS.indexOf(",",start); 
		var paperlessFlag = ""; 
        if(start&gt;0 &amp;&amp; end!=0) paperlessFlag = contextFromLS.substring(start+14, end);      
        start = contextFromLS.indexOf("iruAuthorized="); 
        end = 0; 
        if(start&gt;0) end = contextFromLS.indexOf(",",start); 
		var iruAuthorized = ""; 
        if(start&gt;0 &amp;&amp; end!=0) iruAuthorized = contextFromLS.substring(start+14, end);              
        var paperlessFlagFromJson = json.paperlessFlag!=null?json.paperlessFlag.toString():""; 
        var iruAuthFlagFromJson = json.iruAuthorized!=null?json.iruAuthorized.toString():"false"; 
		//Loading Profile data from Lower Funnel to upper funnel profile object 
		if(sessionStorage.ufProfile !==undefined){ 
    	  window.sessionStorage.setItem('profile', JSON.stringify(jQuery.extend(JSON.parse(window.sessionStorage.profile) , JSON.parse(window.sessionStorage.ufProfile)))); 
		} 
		//mapping required check availability properties to atgprofile  
		if(sessionStorage.ufProfile !== undefined &amp;&amp; jQuery.isEmptyObject(json)){ 
			var LFJson = jQuery.parseJSON(sessionStorage.ufProfile); 
			json.ban = LFJson.uverseAccounts[0].ban; 
			json.loginId = LFJson.loginId; 
			json.state = LFJson.profile.state; 
			json.city = LFJson.profile.city; 
			json.zip5 = LFJson.profile.zipCode; 
			json.addressId = LFJson.profile.addressId; 
			json.dma = LFJson.profile.dma; 
			json.checkAvailabilityPerformed = "Y"; 
			json.addressLine1 = LFJson.profile.addressLine1; 
			json.addressLine2 = LFJson.profile.addressLine2; 
			json.customerState = 'authenticated'; 
            json.cState = 'authenticated'; 
			json.existUverse = true; 
			json.uverseQual = LFJson.profile.isUverseAvailable  ? "Y" : "N"; 
			json.uHSIAQual = LFJson.profile.isHSIAAvailable  ? "Y" : "N"; 
			json.uVOIPQual = LFJson.profile.isVOIPAvailable  ? "Y" : "N"; 
			json.uIPTVQual = LFJson.profile.isIPTVAvailable  ? "Y" : "N"; 
			//json.maxHsiaSpeed = LFJson.CkavDataBean.maxHsiaSpeedAvailable; 
			json.maxUverseSpeed = LFJson.CkavDataBean.maxHsiaSpeedAvailable; 
			if(json.maxUverseSpeed === null){ 
                json.maxUverseSpeed = ""; 
            } 
			json.accountType = LFJson.loginType; 
			json.uverseBuyflowMyATTSales = true; 
			json.uZip = LFJson.profile.zipCode; 
        } 
        //Reload local Storage only upon authenticated flow or check availability flow 
        if((json.checkAvailabilityPerformed === 'Y' &amp;&amp; (capFromLS != 'Y' || addressLine1FromLS != json.addressLine1))  
            || json.customerState === 'authenticated'  || json.cState === 'authenticated' 
            || (json.zip5 != null &amp;&amp; json.zip5 != zip5)  
            || (json.zip != null &amp;&amp; json.zip != zip)  
            || paperlessFlagFromJson != paperlessFlag 
            || iruAuthFlagFromJson != iruAuthorized){ 
            console.log('DEBUG: Overwriting LS'); 
            $CQ.each(json, function(key, val) {       
                   var value = val; 
                   if(typeof val=="boolean" || typeof val=="number"){ 
                       value = val.toString(); 
                    } 
                    if(value.indexOf("|")&gt;0){ 
                        value = value.replace(/[|]/g,"~"); 
                    } 
                    if (key === 'region_code') { 
                         key = 'state'; 
                     } 
                    if (key === 'zip') { 
                         value = value.substring(0,5); 
                     } 
                     if (key === 'network') { 
                         if (val === 'att') { 
                             key = 'existDSL'; 
                             value = 'true'; 
                             CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty('compISP', 'false'); 
                         } else { 
                             key = 'existDSL'; 
                             value = 'false'; 
                             CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty('compISP', 'true');                      
                         } 
                     } 
            //set Ready2Go value from ORDER_COOKIE, instead of profile because of order summary session invalidation limitation. 
            if (key == 'existR2G') { 
                         var orderCookie = ATT.util.getCookie('ORDER_COOKIE'); 
                         if(orderCookie) { 
                             var orderCookieJson = jQuery.parseJSON(orderCookie); 
                             value = orderCookieJson.R2GExists; 
                         } 
                     } 
                CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty(key, value);                     
            }); 
        } 
		if(window.location.href.indexOf('suppress_redirect') !== -1) { 
		    CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty("existingUverseCustomer", false); 
		} 
 	// setting browser and operating system after reading from the client side 
         CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty("browser", BrowserDetect.browser);  
         CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty("os", BrowserDetect.OS); 
         //B2C-226133 -Setting localstorage value that is coming from atg profile json 
         CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty("checkAvailabilityPerformed", json.checkAvailabilityPerformed); 
         CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty("flowIndicator", json.flowIndicator); 
         var chkavlPerformed = json.checkAvailabilityPerformed; 
         if (chkavlPerformed === '') {	 
         	CQ_Analytics.ProfileDataMgr.setProperty('welcomeBackUser', 'Y'); 
         } 
         clearTimeout(atgProfileDataTimer); 
         atgProfileDataReady.resolve(data); 
 	}}); 
     }
   </script>
  </div>

     var listViewType = ''; 
		var wirelessDeviceFilterSize = 0; 
		var wirelessDeviceFilterCount = 0; 
		ATT.listPage.showMoreSize = false; 
		ATT.listPage.productListDiv = "#deviceLayout";

		//New code 
		function toggleToDeviceLine() { 
			var listViewType = 'line'; 
			jQuery('#viewLineIconDeselected').css('display','none');  
			jQuery('#viewLineIconSelected').css('display','block'); 
			jQuery('#viewGridIconSelected').css('display','none');  
			jQuery('#viewGridIconDeselected').css('display','block');  
			window.localStorage.setItem(ATT.listPage.pageName() + "ViewPref", listViewType); 
			jQuery("#uniformStyle").removeClass("gridView").addClass("lineView"); 
		} 
		function toggleToDeviceGrid() { 
			var listViewType = 'grid'; 
			jQuery('#viewLineIconDeselected').css('display','block');  
			jQuery('#viewLineIconSelected').css('display','none');  
			jQuery('#viewGridIconSelected').css('display','block');  
			jQuery('#viewGridIconDeselected').css('display','none');  
			window.localStorage.setItem(ATT.listPage.pageName() + "ViewPref", listViewType); 
			jQuery("#uniformStyle").removeClass("lineView").addClass("gridView"); 
		} 
		jQuery(document).ready(function() { 
			var vArray = jQuery("input[type=radio]");                     
			var filetrDefault = 'LG'; 
			if(filetrDefault != null &amp;&amp; filetrDefault.length &gt; 0)    
			{ 
				 for (var i=0; i&lt;vArray.length; i++) { 
					var position = vArray[i].value.toLowerCase().indexOf(filetrDefault.toLowerCase()) ; 
					if ((position != -1) &amp;&amp; (vArray[i].checked == true)) 
					{ 
						jQuery("#"+ vArray[i].id).click();  
					} 
				} 
			} 
		});
    </script>

                <script type="text/javascript">
                 //hiding child filter on page load 
jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 
	jQuery("#taxoManu input").each(function(){ 
		if(jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") != "" ){ 
			var divToHide = jQuery(this).attr("childFilter"); 
            console.log(divToHide); 
			if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("checked").parent().attr("class", "");  
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("default"); 
			} 
			if(!jQuery(this).is(':checked')){ 
				if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
					jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).hide(); 
					jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("checked").parent().attr("class", ""); 
				} 
			}   
			else 
				jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).insertAfter(jQuery(this).closest("form"));                      
		} 
	});  
    jQuery("#taxoManu input").click(function(){showChild(this.id);});  
    jQuery("#taxoManu a").each(function(){  
		if(jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") != "" ){ 
			var divToHide = jQuery(this).attr("childFilter"); 
			if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("a").attr("class", "listFilterGroup");  
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("a").removeAttr("default"); 
			} 
            if(!jQuery(this).hasClass('focus')){ 
				if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
                    jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).hide(); 
				} 
			}   
            else{  
                jQuery("#div_"+divToHide+" ul").insertAfter(jQuery(this));  
            } 
		} 
	}); 
	jQuery("#taxoManu a").click(function(){showChild(this.id);});   
});
                </script>
               </div>

                <script type="text/javascript">
                 //hiding child filter on page load 
jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 
    jQuery("#rangePricing input").each(function(){ 
        if(jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") != "" ){ 
            var divToHide = jQuery(this).attr("childFilter"); 
             if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
                jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("checked").parent().attr("class", "");  
                jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("default"); 
             } 
            if(!jQuery(this).is(':checked')){ 
                if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
                    jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).hide(); 
                    jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("checked").parent().attr("class", ""); 
                } 
            }   
            else 
                jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).insertAfter(jQuery(this).closest("form"));                      
        }         
    });  
    jQuery("#rangePricing input").click(function(){showChild(this.id);});   
});
                </script>

                <script type="text/javascript">
                 //hiding child filter on page load 
jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 
	jQuery("#skuCondition input").each(function(){ 
		if(jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") != "" ){ 
			var divToHide = jQuery(this).attr("childFilter"); 
            console.log(divToHide); 
			if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("checked").parent().attr("class", "");  
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("default"); 
			} 
			if(!jQuery(this).is(':checked')){ 
				if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
					jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).hide(); 
					jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("checked").parent().attr("class", ""); 
				} 
			}   
			else 
				jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).insertAfter(jQuery(this).closest("form"));                      
		} 
	});  
    jQuery("#skuCondition input").click(function(){showChild(this.id);});  
    jQuery("#skuCondition a").each(function(){  
		if(jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") != "" ){ 
			var divToHide = jQuery(this).attr("childFilter"); 
			if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("a").attr("class", "listFilterGroup");  
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("a").removeAttr("default"); 
			} 
            if(!jQuery(this).hasClass('focus')){ 
				if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
                    jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).hide(); 
				} 
			}   
            else{  
                jQuery("#div_"+divToHide+" ul").insertAfter(jQuery(this));  
            } 
		} 
	}); 
	jQuery("#skuCondition a").click(function(){showChild(this.id);});   
});
                </script>
               </div>

                <script type="text/javascript">
                 //hiding child filter on page load 
jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 
	jQuery("#taxoFeatures input").each(function(){ 
		if(jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") != "" ){ 
			var divToHide = jQuery(this).attr("childFilter"); 
            console.log(divToHide); 
			if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("checked").parent().attr("class", "");  
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("default"); 
			} 
			if(!jQuery(this).is(':checked')){ 
				if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
					jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).hide(); 
					jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).find("input").removeAttr("checked").parent().attr("class", ""); 
				} 
			}   
			else 
				jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).insertAfter(jQuery(this).closest("form"));                      
		} 
	});  
    jQuery("#taxoFeatures input").click(function(){showChild(this.id);});  
    jQuery("#taxoFeatures a").each(function(){  
		if(jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).attr("childFilter") != "" ){ 
			var divToHide = jQuery(this).attr("childFilter"); 
			if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("a").attr("class", "listFilterGroup");  
				jQuery("#"+divToHide).find("a").removeAttr("default"); 
			} 
            if(!jQuery(this).hasClass('focus')){ 
				if(jQuery("#"+divToHide).length){ 
                    jQuery("#div_"+divToHide).hide(); 
				} 
			}   
            else{  
                jQuery("#div_"+divToHide+" ul").insertAfter(jQuery(this));  
            } 
		} 
	}); 
	jQuery("#taxoFeatures a").click(function(){showChild(this.id);});   
});
                </script>

          <script type="text/javascript">
           function updateCompatibilityMessage(){ 
								var compatibilityMessage, cartContents, planName; 
								compatibilityMessage = "Viewing all devices compatible with: {plan name}"; 
								cartContents = ATT.globalVars.cartContents; 
								planName = cartContents.planInContextName; 
								if(cartContents.cartIsEmpty &amp;&amp; planName == ""){ 
									jQuery("#compatibilityMessage").html("").hide(); 
									return; 
								} 
								if(!!planName){ 
									jQuery("#yellowMessage").show(); 
									jQuery("#compatibilityMessage").html(compatibilityMessage.replace("{0}",planName).replace("{plan name}","&lt;strong&gt;" + planName + "&lt;/strong&gt;")); 
									if(!jQuery("#filterTokens div").length){jQuery("#filterAttributeDisplay").hide()} 
								} 
							} 
							jQuery.when(ATT.globalVars.cartPromise).done(updateCompatibilityMessage);
          </script>

              <script type="text/javascript">
               jQuery(document).ready(function ($) { 
	    	jQuery(".swatch").click(function(){ 
		    	var cskuid = $(this).attr('id'); 
		    	var parentVal = jQuery(this).closest('.list-item'); 
		    	var parentValID = jQuery(this).closest('.list-item').attr('id'); 
		    	var accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.titleURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	var presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.rtngURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		    	var presentHrefSplit = presentHref.split('#sku='); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("?sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHrefSplit[0]+"#tab4?sku="+cskuid); 
		        }  
		    	accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.imageURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.btnURLchng').attr('id');	 
		        jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		        presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
	    	}); 
	    });
              </script>

	    	jQuery(".swatch").click(function(){ 
		    	var cskuid = $(this).attr('id'); 
		    	var parentVal = jQuery(this).closest('.list-item'); 
		    	var parentValID = jQuery(this).closest('.list-item').attr('id'); 
		    	var accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.titleURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	var presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.rtngURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		    	var presentHrefSplit = presentHref.split('#sku='); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("?sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHrefSplit[0]+"#tab4?sku="+cskuid); 
		        }  
		    	accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.imageURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.btnURLchng').attr('id');	 
		        jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		        presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
	    	}); 
	    });

	    	jQuery(".swatch").click(function(){ 
		    	var cskuid = $(this).attr('id'); 
		    	var parentVal = jQuery(this).closest('.list-item'); 
		    	var parentValID = jQuery(this).closest('.list-item').attr('id'); 
		    	var accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.titleURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	var presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.rtngURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		    	var presentHrefSplit = presentHref.split('#sku='); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("?sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHrefSplit[0]+"#tab4?sku="+cskuid); 
		        }  
		    	accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.imageURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.btnURLchng').attr('id');	 
		        jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		        presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
	    	}); 
	    });

               jQuery(document).ready(function ($) { 
	    	jQuery(".swatch").click(function(){ 
		    	var cskuid = $(this).attr('id'); 
		    	var parentVal = jQuery(this).closest('.list-item'); 
		    	var parentValID = jQuery(this).closest('.list-item').attr('id'); 
		    	var accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.titleURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	var presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.rtngURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		    	var presentHrefSplit = presentHref.split('#sku='); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("?sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHrefSplit[0]+"#tab4?sku="+cskuid); 
		        }  
		    	accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.imageURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.btnURLchng').attr('id');	 
		        jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		        presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
	    	}); 
	    });
              </script>

		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.rtngURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		    	var presentHrefSplit = presentHref.split('#sku='); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("?sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHrefSplit[0]+"#tab4?sku="+cskuid); 
		        }  
		    	accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.imageURLchng').attr('id'); 
		    	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		    	presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
		        accessOnID = $('#'+parentValID).find('.btnURLchng').attr('id');	 
		        jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('data-cskuid',cskuid); 
		        presentHref = jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href'); 
		        if(presentHref.indexOf("#sku=") &lt; 0){ 
		        	jQuery('#'+accessOnID).attr('href',presentHref+"#sku="+cskuid); 
		        } 
	    	}); 
	    });
              </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       function resetView(){ 
			var foo = window.localStorage.getItem(ATT.listPage.pageName() + "ViewPref") == "line" ? toggleToDeviceLine() : toggleToDeviceGrid(); 
		} 
		function refreshProducts(forceRefresh){ 
			if(forceRefresh || ATT.util.attPLCookie() || !!ATT.globalVars.cartContents.userZip){ 
				ATT.listPage.getItemInfo(); 
				return true; 
			} 
		} 
		function setCurrentCommitmentTerm () { 
			var changed = false; 
			var vCurrentCommitmentTerm = ''; 
			if (vCurrentCommitmentTerm != '') { 
				var vCommitmentTerm = document.getElementsByName("commitmentTerm"); 
				for (var i=0; i&lt;vCommitmentTerm.length; i++) { 
					if (vCommitmentTerm[i].value == vCurrentCommitmentTerm){ 
						vCommitmentTerm[i].checked = true; 
						//ATT.listPage.getItemInfo(); 
						jQuery.uniform.update('.listFilterGroup'); 
						changed = true; 
					} 
				} 
			} 
			return changed; //did we get a new set? 
		} // end of setCurrentCommitmentTerm 
		jQuery.when(ATT.globalVars.cartPromise).done(function(){ 
			var listSize, listSizePref, defaultView, needNewView, updateCommitmentFlag, gotNewSet, timerIsON; 
			jQuery(document).ready(function(){ 
			ATT.listPage.initStickyNav(); 
			ATT.listPage.initInfiniteScroll(); 
			}); 
			ATT.listPage.onComplete = resetView; 
			resetView(); 
			//get stored preferences and determine if we need to force a refresh 
			listSizePref = ATT.listPage.getShowMorePref(); 
			listSize = jQuery('input#showMore').attr('value'); 
			defaultView = ATT.listPage.constructUserSpecificUrl('/shop/wireless/devices/lg.deviceListView.xhr.html','ALL', 'postpaid'); 
			timerIsON = String(ATT.globalVars.cartContents.globalTimerPricingOn) == "true"; 
			updateCommitmentFlag = setCurrentCommitmentTerm(); 
			gotNewSet = false; 
			if(listSizePref != listSize){needNewView = true; jQuery('input#showMore').attr('value', listSizePref)} 
			var v_buyFlowType= 'NEW';	 
	        if (v_buyFlowType === 'NEW') { 
				ATT.listPage.setUrl(defaultView); 
				ATT.listPage.setDivId('deviceLayout'); 
			} 
			gotNewSet = ATT.listPage.setFilter();  
			if (!gotNewSet || needNewView || timerIsON){ 
				gotNewSet = refreshProducts(needNewView); 
			} 
            if (v_buyFlowType === 'NEW') { 
           		jQuery('#shoppingassistant').load('/shop/wireless/devices/lg.shoppingassistant.xhr.html?pageType=deviceList&amp;paymentType=postpaid&amp;deviceType=ALL&amp;planType=&amp;sku='); 
            }				 
		});
      </script>

   function openErrorModal(errorMessage){ 
	jQuery.colorbox({'open':true, 'inline':true, href:"#onlyModelContent #failureModal", width:520, scrolling:false, onComplete:function(){modalUtils.init();jQuery.colorbox.resize();}}); 
		jQuery('#ok_retain').live('click', function () {		 
			jQuery.colorbox.close()  
		});	 
	} 
	var errorMsgBuyFlow = "We're sorry, but the device you chose isn't available. Please choose another device to continue with your order."; 
	jQuery(document).ready(function ($) { 
		var isAquisitionFilterApplied = false; 
		$(document).ajaxStop(function(){ 
			if (ATT.globalVars.cartContents.isValidAccessCardHolder) { 
				$('.listGrid-upEligibility').hide(); 
				if(isAquisitionFilterApplied === false){ 
					//Apply Filter Criteria for Citi Aquisition Flow 
					filterCriteriaForAquisition(); 
					//Display Citi Banner 
					$("#citiBanner").show(); 
					isAquisitionFilterApplied = true; 
				} 
			} 
		}); 
		$("#citiBanner").click(function() {  
			$.colorbox({ 
				href: '/shop/en/wireless/modals/citibank_legal_disclaimer_modal.html', 
				iframe: false, 
				scrolling: false, 
				width: 700, 
				onComplete: (function(){ 
					$(".closeModal").click(function (event) { 
						$.colorbox.close(); 
					}); 
				}) 
			}); 
		}); 
		var title = $('#citiBanner').attr("title"); 
		$('#citiBanner').mouseover(function() { 
			$(this).attr("tmp_title", title); 
			// Set the title to nothing so we don't see the tooltips 
			$(this).attr("title",""); 
		}).mouseout( 
		function() { 
		$(this).attr('title', title); 
		$(this).attr("tmp_title", ""); 
		}); 
		/* Retain Cart Implementation start */ 
		var v_isRetainCartContantsAvl = $('#retainCartStatusID').data('retainCartStatus');  
		var v_isRetainCartConflictType = $('#retainCartConflictTypeID').data('retainCartConflictType'); 
		if(v_isRetainCartConflictType != null &amp;&amp; v_isRetainCartConflictType != '' &amp;&amp; v_isRetainCartConflictType != 'NO_CONFLICT'){ 
			ATT.FEM.display.dialogBox('',errorMsgBuyFlow ,'',false); 
		} 
		if (v_isRetainCartContantsAvl == true){ 
			$.when(ATT.globalVars.cartPromise).done(function(){ 
				$( ".addToCart" ).trigger( "click" ); 
			}); 
			return; 
		} 
		/* Retain Cart Implementation End */ 
		var buyflow = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
		/* Error modal is displayed when retain device/plan fails*/ 
		var errorMsg = $('#fscenarioCode').text(); 
		if(errorMsg){ 
			if(buyflow=='AL'){ 
			ATT.FEM.display.dialogBox('',errorMsg ,'',false); 
			} else if(buyflow=='UP'){ 
				/* ATT.FEM.display.dialogBox('',errorMsg ,'',false); */ 
				openErrorModal(errorMsg); 
			}  
		}  
		ATT.ui.rtiListOOS.oosVar.outofstock = 'OUT OF STOCK'; 
		ATT.ui.rtiListOOS.oosVar.url = '/shop/wireless/devices/lg.outofstockskus.html'; 
		ATT.ui.rtiListOOS.oosVar.list = 'device'; 
		ATT.ui.rtiListOOS.init(); 
		var v_hash = location.hash.substr(1).toLowerCase(); 
		if (v_hash == 'next') { 
			$('input[value="lease20"]').attr('checked', 'checked'); 
			$('input[value="lease20"]').trigger('click'); 
		} 
		// ECOM14-1255: Default Contract Length Filter to Next 18 for UP and AL Flow 
		var deviceType = 'ALL'; 
		var selectedFilters = 0; 
		if((/(AL)/).test(buyflow) &amp;&amp; window.localStorage.getItem("FilterQueryString")!=null ) 
		{				 
			var filterQueryString = window.localStorage.getItem("FilterQueryString"); 
			if(filterQueryString.length &gt; 0) 
			{ 
				window.localStorage.removeItem("FilterQueryString"); 
				var filterQueryStringArray = filterQueryString.split("&amp;");	 
				for(i=0;i &lt; filterQueryStringArray.length;i++) 
				{ 
					var filtervalue= filterQueryStringArray[i].split("=")[1]; 
					var input = "\'input[value=\"" + filtervalue + "\"]\'"; 
					if(jQuery(input)) 
					{ 
						jQuery(input).attr('checked', 'checked'); 
						jQuery(input).trigger('click'); 
						jQuery(input).attr('checked', 'checked'); 
						selectedFilters = 1; 
					} 
				} 
			} 
		} 
		//QC42801 Setting local storage value for freephones 
		var currentPageUrl = window.location.href.substr(window.location.href.lastIndexOf("/")+1); 
		var currentPage = currentPageUrl.split('.'); 
		if((currentPage[0] == 'freephones')){ 
			var qString = "commitmentTerm=24&amp;showMoreListSize=12"; 
			jQuery('#commitmentTerm1').trigger('click'); 
			window.localStorage.setItem(ATT.listPage.getCookieName(),ATT.util.getCookie("SHOPSESSIONID") + ";"+qString); 
		} 
		// QC#14149 Removing default style for taxostyle 
		var taxoStyleParam = getURLParam("taxoStyle"); 
		if(taxoStyleParam != ""){ 
			jQuery('#uniform-taxoStyle1').find('span').removeClass('checked');	 
		} 
		if(selectedFilters == 0) 
		{ 
			var defaultInstallTerm = $("#v_defaultInstallCommitTerm").val(); 
			var defaultNextTerm = $("#v_defaultNextCommitTerm").val(); 
			var deviceTabGroupType = $("#v_deviceTabGroupType").val(); 
			var leaseTerm = getURLParam("commitmentTerm"); 
			var identifierMap = $("#v_identifierMap").val(); 
			var defaultTerm = '24'; 
			if((deviceTabGroupType == 'Cellphone' || deviceType == 'Cellphone') &amp;&amp; (deviceType != 'ALL')){ 
				defaultTerm = defaultNextTerm; 
			} 
			else if((deviceTabGroupType == 'Tablet' || deviceType == 'Tablet') &amp;&amp; (deviceType != 'ALL')){ 
				defaultTerm = defaultInstallTerm; 
			} 
			else if(deviceTabGroupType == 'Cellphone' &amp;&amp; deviceType == 'ALL'){ 
				defaultTerm = defaultNextTerm; 
			} 
			else if(deviceTabGroupType == 'Tablet' &amp;&amp; deviceType == 'ALL'){ 
				defaultTerm = defaultInstallTerm; 
			} 
			else if(deviceTabGroupType == 'MobileBroadband'){ 
				defaultTerm = 'ALL'; 
			} 
			if(leaseTerm != ""){ 
				var arrOfLeaseLabels = identifierMap.split('|'); 
				var isFirstRadio = false; 
				if(deviceType == 'Cellphone' || deviceType == 'ALL'){ 
					if(jQuery.inArray(leaseTerm, arrOfLeaseLabels) &gt; -1) 
					{ 
						isFirstRadio = true; 
					} 
				} 
				var isChecked = false; 
				jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").each(function(e){ 
					if(deviceType == 'Cellphone' || deviceType == 'ALL'){ 
						if(jQuery(this).val() == leaseTerm || isFirstRadio ){ 
							if(isFirstRadio &amp;&amp; !isChecked) 
							{  
								jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").attr('checked',''); 
								jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").parent('span').removeClass('checked'); 
								jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").attr('checked', 'checked'); 
								jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").parent('span').addClass('checked'); 
								jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").val(leaseTerm); 
								isChecked =true; 
								jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").trigger('click'); 
							} 
							else if(jQuery(this).val() == leaseTerm &amp;&amp; !isChecked) 
							{ 
								jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").attr('checked',''); 
								jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").parent('span').removeClass('checked'); 
								jQuery(this).val(leaseTerm); 
								jQuery(this).attr('checked', 'checked'); 
								jQuery(this).parent('span').addClass('checked'); 
								isChecked = true; 
								jQuery(this).trigger('click'); 
							} 
						} 
						else if(!isChecked) 
						{ 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").attr('checked',''); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").parent('span').removeClass('checked'); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").attr('checked', 'checked'); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").parent('span').addClass('checked'); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").val(defaultTerm); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").trigger('click'); 
						} 
					} 
					else if(deviceType == 'Tablet' || deviceType == 'MobileBroadband') 
					{ 
						if(jQuery(this).val() == leaseTerm &amp;&amp; !isChecked) 
						{ 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").attr('checked',''); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").parent('span').removeClass('checked'); 
							jQuery(this).val(leaseTerm); 
							jQuery(this).attr('checked', 'checked'); 
							jQuery(this).parent('span').addClass('checked'); 
							isChecked =true; 
							jQuery(this).trigger('click'); 
						} 
						else if(!isChecked) 
						{ 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").attr('checked',''); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]").parent('span').removeClass('checked'); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").attr('checked', 'checked'); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").parent('span').addClass('checked'); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").val(defaultTerm); 
							jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").trigger('click'); 
						} 
					} 
				}); 
			} 
			else 
			{ 
				// If Urlparam doesn't have commitmentTerm and then 
				// Choose Installment-Plan as the default selection for tablet filter  
				if(!(typeof ATT.listPage.getCookieName == "function" &amp;&amp; window.localStorage.getItem(ATT.listPage.getCookieName()) != "" &amp;&amp; window.localStorage.getItem(ATT.listPage.getCookieName()) != undefined &amp;&amp; (window.localStorage.getItem(ATT.listPage.getCookieName()).indexOf("commitmentTerm") != -1) )) 
				{ 
					jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").attr('checked', 'checked'); 
					jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").parent('span').addClass('checked'); 
					jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").val(defaultTerm); 
					jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").trigger('click'); 
				} 
			} 
			// QC#21148 Retaining filter selection in between devicelist and devicedetails page 
			var qStr = "commitmentTerm="+leaseTerm+"&amp;showMoreListSize=12"; 
			if (typeof (Storage) !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; leaseTerm !="") { // check if web storage is browser supported 
				window.localStorage.setItem(ATT.listPage.getCookieName(),ATT.util.getCookie("SHOPSESSIONID") + ";"+qStr); 
			} 
			ATT.listPage.generateFilterTokens(); 
			// ATTDF.load(); 
		} 
		if ((/(UP)/).test(buyflow)) { 
			if(selectedFilters == 0) 
			{ 
				var Upgelg = window.localStorage.getItem("selectedMRECode"); 
				if (deviceType == 'Tablet' &amp;&amp; jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").val() == $("#v_defaultInstallCommitTerm").val()) { 
					jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").attr('checked', 'checked');

					jQuery('input[value="24"]').trigger('click'); 
				} 
				else if((Upgelg=="LTV809" || Upgelg=="LTV811" || Upgelg=="LTV804" || Upgelg=="LTV806" || Upgelg=="LTV807")){ 
					   jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").attr('checked', 'checked');  
						jQuery("#div_commitmentTerm input[type=radio]:first").trigger('click'); 
				} 
				else if(Upgelg=="LTV0801" || Upgelg=="LTV0808" || Upgelg=="LTV805" || Upgelg=="LTV0810"){ 
					jQuery('input[value="1"]').attr('checked', 'checked'); 
					jQuery('input[value="1"]').trigger('click'); 
				} 
			} 
		} 
		/* Alert modal is displayed when authenticated customer bookmark - Join group page*/ 
		var authCustRedn = ATT.DeviceList.getParameterByName('acrd'); 
		if(authCustRedn) { 
			$.colorbox({html:'&lt;div class="modalHeader"&gt;&lt;h1&gt;Important Information&lt;/h1&gt;&lt;a href="#Close" class="closeModal"&gt;Close&lt;/a&gt;'+ 
				'&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style="padding:25px;"&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;p&gt;Please add a device to your cart to continue.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;', width:520, onComplete:function(){modalUtils.init();jQuery.colorbox.resize();}}); 
		} 
		if(getURLParam("commitmentTerm")){ 
			jQuery("input[type=radio][class=listFilterGroup]:checked").click(); 
		} 
	}); 
	ATT.namespace('DeviceList'); 
	ATT.DeviceList = (function ($) { 
		var getParameterByName; 
		getParameterByName = function (name) { 
			return decodeURIComponent((new RegExp('[?|&amp;]' + name + '=' + '([^&amp;;]+?)(&amp;|#|;|$)').exec(location.search)||[,""])[1].replace(/\+/g, '%20'))||null; 
		}; 
		return { 
			getParameterByName: getParameterByName 
		}; 
	}(jQuery)); 
	/* Modal to open on Click of See offer or See price Details */ 
	jQuery(".devicelegal").live("click", ATT.listPage.showseeofferLegal);
  </script>

	ATT.globalVars.paymentType = function(){ 
		var wtPaymentMethod; 
		switch ("creditCard") { 
		case ("billToAccount"): 
			wtPaymentMethod = "Bill To Account"; 
            return wtPaymentMethod; 
			break; 
		case ("creditCard"): 
			wtPaymentMethod = "New CC"; 
            return wtPaymentMethod; 
			break; 
		case ("paymentProfile"): 
			wtPaymentMethod = "Payment Profile"; 
            return wtPaymentMethod; 
			break; 
		default: 
			wtPaymentMethod = "0"; 
            return wtPaymentMethod; 
			break; 
		}

   <script>
    ATT.globalVars.localStorageSetup = function () { 
		//to view output of ATT.log set ATT.util.setCookie('attdebug','true',1); 
	    console.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: document for localStorageSetup is ready!'); 
	    var rightnow = new Date(); 
	    rightnow.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0); 
	    var compareToday = JSON.stringify(rightnow); 
	    var compareTodayObj = JSON.parse(compareToday); 
	    ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: today is: ' + compareTodayObj); 
	    // set number of days to expire 
	    var label_interval = parseInt('30'); // label.lpvisitortype.numberofdaystoexpir 
	    var interval = 30; //in case this value is not set by authoring  label 
	    if (!label_interval || isNaN(label_interval)) { 
	        var label_interval = 30; 
	    } 
	    if (localStorage.getItem("visitorTypeKey") === null) { 
	        var startDate = new Date(); 
	        startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0); 
	        var expiresDate = new Date(); 
	        expiresDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0); 
	        expiresDate.setDate(expiresDate.getDate() + label_interval); 
	        var objectRET = { 
	            valueObjKey: "RET", 
	            startdateObjKey: startDate, 
	            expdateObjKey: expiresDate 
	        }; 
	        localStorage.setItem("visitorTypeKey", JSON.stringify(objectRET)); 
	        ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
	        lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType || 'UNK']); 
	        ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: creating local storage object with start date:' + startDate + ' and expiration date: ' + expiresDate); 
	    } else { 
	        /* if key exists then create vars below */ 
	        var localStorageObj = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("visitorTypeKey")); 
	        var ExpirationDateObj = localStorageObj.expdateObjKey; 
	        var StartDateObj = localStorageObj.startdateObjKey; 
	        var localStorageVisitorType = localStorageObj.valueObjKey; //this value is always RET	} 
	        ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: Found local storage object with the following values: '); 
	        ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: start Date: ' + StartDateObj); 
	        ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: expiration Date: ' + ExpirationDateObj); 
	        if (typeof (Storage) !== "undefined") { // check if web storage is browser supported 
	            ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: web storage supported!!!"); 
	            if ((ATT.globalVars.cartContents.authenticated === "authenticated" &amp;&amp; ATT.globalVars.cartContents.wirelessAuthenticated === true) || (StartDateObj == compareTodayObj) || (ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowTypeShown === true)) { //visitor type is not RET 
	                localStorage.userName = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
	                ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
	                ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: setting visitorType to NEW, AL, ALF or UP"); 
	                lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType || 'UNK']); 
	            } else { //visitor type is RET 
	                localStorage.userName = localStorageVisitorType; 
	                ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: setting visitorType to RET"); 
	                ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = localStorageVisitorType; 
	                lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType || 'UNK']); 
	            } 
	            //  ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = localStorageVisitorType; 
	            if (localStorage.getItem("visitorTypeKey") === null) {} else { 
	                if (ExpirationDateObj &gt; compareTodayObj) { 
	                    ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: visitorTypeKey storage object is not expired"); 
	                } else { 
	                    localStorage.removeItem("visitorTypeKey"); 
	                    ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: visitorTypeKey storage object expired and deleting it from local storage ... setting visitor type to NEW"); 
	                    ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
	                    lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType || 'UNK']); 
	                } //remove the localstorage key and reset it 
	            } 
	            ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: FINAL VALUE IS: " + ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType); 
	        } else { 
	            localStorage.userName = "UNK"; 
	            ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
	            ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: Browser does not support Web Storage"); 
	            lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType || 'UNK']); 
	            ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: FINAL VALUE IS: " + ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType); 
	        } 
	    } 
	};
   </script>
   <script>
    ATT.globalVars.localStorageSetup = function () { 
		//to view output of ATT.log set ATT.util.setCookie('attdebug','true',1); 
		console.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: document for localStorageSetup is ready!'); 
		var rightnow = new Date(); 
		rightnow.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0); 
		var compareToday = JSON.stringify(rightnow); 
		var compareTodayObj = JSON.parse(compareToday); 
		ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: today is: ' + compareTodayObj); 
		// set number of days to expire 
		var label_interval = parseInt('30'); // label.lpvisitortype.numberofdaystoexpir 
		var interval = 30; //in case this value is not set by authoring  label 
		if (!label_interval || isNaN(label_interval)) { 
			var label_interval = 30; 
		} 
		if (localStorage.getItem("visitorTypeKey") === null) { 
			var startDate = new Date(); 
			startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0); 
			var expiresDate = new Date(); 
			expiresDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0); 
			expiresDate.setDate(expiresDate.getDate() + label_interval); 
			var objectRET = { 
				valueObjKey: "RET", 
				startdateObjKey: startDate, 
				expdateObjKey: expiresDate 
			}; 
			localStorage.setItem("visitorTypeKey", JSON.stringify(objectRET)); 
			ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
			lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType || 'UNK']); 
			ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: creating local storage object with start date:' + startDate + ' and expiration date: ' + expiresDate); 
		} else { 
			/* if key exists then create vars below */ 
			var localStorageObj = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("visitorTypeKey")); 
			var ExpirationDateObj = localStorageObj.expdateObjKey; 
			var StartDateObj = localStorageObj.startdateObjKey; 
			var localStorageVisitorType = localStorageObj.valueObjKey; //this value is always RET	} 
			ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: Found local storage object with the following values: '); 
			ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: start Date: ' + StartDateObj); 
			ATT.log('LP VISITOR TYPE: expiration Date: ' + ExpirationDateObj); 
			if (typeof (Storage) !== "undefined") { // check if web storage is browser supported 
				ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: web storage supported!!!"); 
				if ((ATT.globalVars.cartContents.authenticated === "authenticated" &amp;&amp; ATT.globalVars.cartContents.wirelessAuthenticated === true) || (StartDateObj == compareTodayObj) || (ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowTypeShown === true)) { //visitor type is not RET 
					localStorage.userName = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
					ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
					ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: setting visitorType to NEW, AL, ALF or UP"); 
					lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType || 'UNK']); 
				} else { //visitor type is RET 
					localStorage.userName = localStorageVisitorType; 
					ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: setting visitorType to RET"); 
					ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = localStorageVisitorType; 
					lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType || 'UNK']); 
				} 
				//  ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = localStorageVisitorType; 
				if (localStorage.getItem("visitorTypeKey") === null) {} else { 
					if (ExpirationDateObj &gt; compareTodayObj) { 
						ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: visitorTypeKey storage object is not expired"); 
					} else { 
						localStorage.removeItem("visitorTypeKey"); 
						ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: visitorTypeKey storage object expired and deleting it from local storage ... setting visitor type to NEW"); 
						ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
						lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType || 'UNK']); 
					} //remove the localstorage key and reset it 
				} 
				ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: FINAL VALUE IS: " + ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType); 
			} else { 
				localStorage.userName = "UNK"; 
				ATT.globalVars.lpVisitorType = ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType; 
				ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: Browser does not support Web Storage"); 
				lpMTagConfig.vars.push(["page", "visitorType", ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType || 'UNK']); 
				ATT.log("LP VISITOR TYPE: FINAL VALUE IS: " + ATT.globalVars.cartContents.buyFlowType); 
			} 
		} 
	};
